*** HOUSE MUSIC ***

Greetings to all my CLUBHOUSE members, listeners, and pioneers!!

I first want to extend a hearty welcome to all my "HOUSEHEADZ", who have joined the CLUBHOUSE regime and supported the site.  Our aims at the CLUBHOUSE is to deliver authentic HOUSE vibes and expose the ecclectic sounds of the underground to the global masses.   

In our continual efforts to promote HOUSE music and provide quality services to our audience,  The entire CLUBHOUSE staff encourages you to email any thoughts, ideas, or suggestions you may have, that will make our aims obtainable.  Please feel free to share with us, the style of HOUSE music you like, your favorite songs/tunes you would like to hear, your favorite mixes on the site, and comments pertaining to the website.

Thanks again for all the love and support... as the CLUBHOUSE team looks forward to bringing more superb mixes and the sounds of the underground to the surface!!

**HOUSE MUSIC EVENT in NEWARK, NJ (LINCOLN PARK) -- FREE EVENT!!!!! **
To all my HOUSE HEADZ...
 
There is an event in North Jersey that is guaranteed to be a sure SMOOOOOOOOKER!!!  Here's a good opportunity to get together with the crew and bug out like in the Oooooold dayz!! Laugh, eat, dance and meditate to some good old-fashioned HOUSE music!!
 
Bring your dancin' shoes, a sweat rag, and plenty of Bengay!! ;-)
(Details below)
 
 
===========================================
Paaaaaaaaarty in the Park!!!!
This event has been talked about as a big hit since it first started two years ago. People come into Newark, NJ from all around the Tri-state area and some even travel in for this event. The first two years the event was a HUGE hit with hundreds of people getting their dance on in the great outdoors of the historic district of Lincoln Park in Newark, NJ. And we will be there too!!!!
The DJ's are none other than:

  • Joaquin 'Joe' Clausell of the infamous Body and Soul team
  • Hippie Torrales formerly of Club Zanzibar
  • Naeem Johnson
  • Omar Abdallah
  • Club Docks


Performances by none other than:

  • Rochelle Fleming formerly of First Choice (You know her: Love Sensation, Let No Man Put Asunder, Love Thang, Dr. Love...)
  • Teddy Douglas featuring Margaret Grace (Very Hot New Producer and Singer with hits like Whatcha Gonna Do)


There will also be a tribute to disco legend Sylvester.
The after party will be at Newark Symphony Hall by the people who bring you the Deliverance Parties.
 
Tickets for the afterparty are $13 in advance at the Newark Symphony Hall Box Office. You can buy tickets at the door for a slightly higher price.
So everybody get your dancing shoes out and park gear ready for one of the best parties of the summer, RAIN or SHINE!!!
 
Lincoln Park is in Newark New Jersey. The park is bordered by Broad Street and Lincoln Park (Clinton St).
